 jaane- kaise phir bal diwas 14 november ko manaaya jane laga
 Children's Day was celebrated on November 20, Children's Day was celebrated since 1925
 jise 1953 main duniya bhar main ise manyata mili
 The United Nations announced the celebration of November 20 as Children's Day, but it is celebrated on different days in other countries
 bharat main bhi pehle yah 20 november ko hi manaaya jaataa tha, lekin 1964 main pradhanmantri jawaharlal nehru ke nidhan (27 may 1964) ke baad sarvasahmati se ye faisla liya gaya ki jawaharlal nehru ke janmdin ko bal diwas ke taur par mana jayega

 1
 First of all, open the suitcase completely on the ground
 2
 Put the socks inside the shoes
 iske baad juuton ko suutakes main sabase pehle rakh den
 This will not lose your socks and won't spoil the shoes either
 3
 Fold thick clothes like jeans, sweaters over the shoes and press them downwards

 4
 agar aapke paas kuch aisa saamaan he jo aasaani se tut saktaa he, to usko suutakes ke bich-bich fold kiye hue kapadon par rakh den

 5
 After this, fold the light clothes like T-shirt, Sakarf and keep it
 6
 It is better to keep the clothes folded in a plastic bag

 7
 belt, roomaal or jaruri chote saamaan ko bachi hui jagah par rakhen

 ) Former acting Chief Justice of Pakistan Rana Bhagwandas passed away
 vah 73 saal ke the or beete kuch samay se biimaar chal rahe the
 He was the only Hindu to serve in the country's top judicial post
 bhagavaandas kaa karachi ke ek nijee aspataal main dil kii beemaari kaa ilaaj chal rahaa tha
 He died on Monday
 bhagavaandas pakistan main supreme court ke pramukh ke taur par kaam karne vaale pehle hindu or duusare gaiyr-muslim nyaayadhish the
 He was a highly respected member of the country's judiciary
 vah 2007 main nyaayik sankat ke dauraan supreme court ke kaaryakari pradhan nyaayadhish the
 When Chief Justice Iftikhar Chaudhary went on a foreign trip in 2005 and 2006, Bhagwandas still succeeded him as the Chief Justice
 vah farvari 2000 se supreme court ke nyaayadhish the
 Bhagwandas also served as the chairman of the Federal Public Service Commission of Pakistan
 sindh praant main larkana jile ke nasirabad main disambar 1942 main janme bhagavaandas ne islamic studies main eme kii degree praapt kii thi or unhen samvidhan or kanoon kaa visheshgy mana jaataa tha
 Bhagwandas practiced for nearly two years before being appointed as a judge in July 1967
 unhen june 1994 main sindh hai court kaa nyaayadhish banaaya gaya tha
 The Sindh High Court in 2002 dismissed the appeal that challenged his appointment to the higher judiciary on the grounds that he was a non-muslim
 raashtrapati mamanun hossain or pradhanmantri navaj sharif ne bhagavaandas ke nidhan par gaharaa dukh vyakt karte hue shok sandesh jari kiye hai
 Prime Minister Sharif praised Justice Bhagwandas' role in serving the country as a Supreme Court judge and said he strongly believed in law and order, democracy and principles
 cabinet ne bhi unke nidhan par shok jataayaa he
 a minute of silence was observed at the beginning of the cabinet meeting

 yah to acha hua ki is dhamaake main koi hataahat nahin hua

 ' Kulbhushan Sudhir Jadhav, an Indian citizen, has been sentenced to death by Pakistan for being an agent of RAW
 bharat sarkaar ne kaha he ki unhen kulbhushan ke thikaane yaa unki haalat ke bare main koi bhi jaankaree nahin he

 ' Union Home Minister Rajnath Singh said that the Government of India is engaged in every effort so that Kulbhushan can be brought back
 unhone kaha ki bharat sarkaar har wo qadam uthaaegi jisase kulbhushan ko nyaay milegaa
 But the Indian government is repeatedly emphasizing that the government has given the request of Conceler Access to Pakistan 13 times in the last one year, but not once did it get permission to meet Kulbhushan
 udhar, pakistan sarkaar tark de rahi he ki usne condishnal acces kii baat bharat ke saamne rakhi thi lekin bharat sarkaar ne use thukraa diya tha
 According to information received from the High Commission of India in Pakistan, Pakistan never gave information about Kulbhushan to India
 condishnal acces kaa koi matlab nahin hota
 The Ministry of External Affairs is in constant touch with the family of Kulbhushan
 sarkaar sena court ke faisale ko chunauti dene ke liye supreme court jane kii taiyaari main he lekin iske alag-alag pahaluon par vichaar jari he
 The Prime Minister's Office told NDTV that the Supreme Court of India and Pakistan operate in the same way
 vahaan bharat apil daayar nahin kar saktaa kyonki, bharat is cese main party nahin he
 Since the Government of India cannot go to court itself, the application will be filed by the people of his family

 Farmers have kept the funeral pyre in their fields and threatened to die if the land is acquired
 alam yah he ki jaise hi prashasnic amala jameen adhigrahan ke liye pahunchataa he, to kisaan parijanon ke saath kirosine kaa tel lekar chita par baith jate hai
